[OBJECT:REACTION]

[REACTION:MAKE_SUNFIRE_GOLD_LARGEDAGGER_ADV]
	[NAME:make a sunfire gold large dagger]
	[ADVENTURE_MODE_ENABLED]
	[BUILDING:CARPENTER:NONE]
	[REAGENT:A:150:BAR:NO_SUBTYPE:METAL:SUNFIRE_GOLD]
	[REAGENT:B:1:NONE:NONE:NONE:NONE]
		[PRESERVE_REAGENT][HAS_EDGE]
	[PRODUCT:100:1:WEAPON:ITEM_WEAPON_DAGGER_LARGE:GET_MATERIAL_FROM_REAGENT:A:NONE]
	[SKILL:FORGE_WEAPON]
	[CATEGORY:ADV_WEAPONRYADV]
	[CATEGORY_NAME:Forge Advanced Weaponry]
	[CATEGORY_DESCRIPTION:Use Bars to forge higher tier Weapons and Ammo. The carpenter's workshop has built in anvil and charcoal.]
